Nouvelle session\n- `tmux attach -t nom` - Attacher session\n- `Ctrl+B d` - DÃ©tacher session\n- `tmux ls` - Lister sessions\n\n### Windows\n- `Ctrl+B c` - Nouvelle fenÃªtre\n- `Ctrl+B n` - FenÃªtre suivante\n- `Ctrl+B p` - FenÃªtre prÃ©cÃ©dente\n- `Ctrl+B ,` - Renommer fenÃªtre\n\n### Panes\n- `Ctrl+B %` - Split vertical\n- `Ctrl+B \"` - Split horizontal\n- `Ctrl+B â†â†’â†‘â†“` - Naviguer entre panes\n- `Ctrl+B z` - Toggle fullscreen pane\n\n## âš¡ Nvim\n\n### Navigation\n- `h j k l` - Gauche, Bas, Haut, Droite\n- `w` - Mot suivant\n- `b` - Mot prÃ©cÃ©dent\n- `gg` - DÃ©but fichier\n- `G` - Fin fichier\n\n### Ã‰dition\n- `i` - Insert mode\n- `ESC` - Normal mode\n- `dd` - Supprimer ligne\n- `yy` - Copier ligne\n- `p` - Coller\n\n### Commandes\n- `:w` - Sauvegarder\n- `:q` - Quitter\n- `:wq` - Sauvegarder et quitter\n- `:q!` - Quitter sans sauvegarder\n\n## ğŸ”— Liens utiles\n- [Tmux Cheat Sheet](https://tmuxcheatsheet.com/)\n- [Nvim Documentation](https://neovim.io/doc/)\n\n---\n\n**Note :** ComplÃ¨te au fur et Ã  mesure que tu te rappelles des commandes !\n\nâœ… CHECKLIST - Downloading instead.');\n        downloadNote();\n    }\n}\n\nğŸ¯ PROCÃ‰DURE CORRECTE\nRefais le test :\n\nRafraÃ®chis la page (Ctrl+F5)\nClick \"âš™ï¸ Configure Vault\"\nChoisis le dossier 00_Inbox sur ton NAS\nÃ‰cris une note\nClick \"ğŸ’¾ Save to Vault\"\nâ†’ Devrait sauvegarder DIRECT sans popup !\n\n\nğŸ’¡ Pour changer le navigateur par dÃ©faut :\nWindows 11 :\n\nSettings (Win + I)\nApps â†’ Default apps\nCherche \"Firefox\" (ou ton browser prÃ©fÃ©rÃ©)\nClick dessus\nClick \"Set default\"\n\nOU plus rapide :\n\nOuvre Firefox\nIl te proposera de devenir par dÃ©faut\nClick \"Yes\" ou \"Set as default\"\n\n\nğŸ§ª TESTE MAINTENANT\nAvec le code corrigÃ© :\n\nConfigure vault = 1 fois\nSave = DIRECT dans 00_Inbox/\nPas de popup supplÃ©mentaire !\n\nÃ‡a marche mieux ? ğŸ”¥\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ¤– Message 517 - Assistant\n\n**ID:** msg-517\n\njavascript// Save note to file system\nasync function saveNote() {\n    const content = editor.value;\n    if (!content.trim()) {\n        alert('Nothing to save!');\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // Si pas de vault configurÃ©, demander de le configurer\n    if (!vaultDirHandle) {\n        alert('Please configure vault first by clicking \"âš™ï¸ Configure Vault\"');\n        const configured = await initVault();\n        if (!configured) {\n            downloadNote();\n            return;\n        }\n    }\n\n    try {\n        // VÃ©rifier qu'on a toujours la permission\n        const permission = await vaultDirHandle.queryPermission({ mode: 'readwrite' });\n        if (permission !== 'granted') {\n            const newPermission = await vaultDirHandle.requestPermission({ mode: 'readwrite' });\n            if (newPermission !== 'granted') {\n                alert('Permission denied. Pas d'accÃ¨s filesystem direct\nâ†’ Pas de hotkeys systÃ¨me\nâ†’ Pas de tray icon\nAvec Electron :\nWidget = Vraie app desktop\nâ†’ FenÃªtre native OS\nâ†’ AccÃ¨s complet filesystem (Node.js)\nâ†’ :\nAspectBrowserElectronEffort migrationUI (HTML/CSS)âœ… Identiqueâœ… Identique0%JavaScript logicâœ… Identiqueâœ… Identique0%File I/OâŒ Download onlyâœ… fs.writeFile()10%Hotkeysâš ï¸ LimitÃ©âœ… FAIT\nâ”œâ”€ Quick Capture (download)\nâ”œâ”€ Quick Reference\nâ””â”€ Hub navigation\n\nPhase 2 (Semaines 3-6) : Features avancÃ©es\nâ”œâ”€ Dashboards\nâ”œâ”€ NAS sync\nâ””â”€ AI synthesis\n\nPhase 3 Simplifier le save (5 min)\nRemplace dans index.html :\nLa fonction saveNote() par cette version clean :\njavascript// Save note (simplified download)\nfunction saveNote() {\n    const content = editor.value;\n    if (!content.trim()) {\n        alert('Nothing to save!');\n        return;\n    }\n\n    const now = new Date();\n    const timestamp = now.toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace('T', '_').replace(/:/g, '-');\n    \n    // Extract title from first heading\n    const firstLine = content.split('\\n')[0];\n    let title = 'note';\n    if (firstLine.startsWith('#')) {\n        title = firstLine.replace(/^#+\\s*/, '').trim()\n            .toLowerCase()\n            .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')\n            .substring(0, 50);\n    }\n    \n    const filename = `${timestamp}_${title}.md`;\n\n    // Download file\n    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/markdown' });\n    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);\n    const a = document.createElement('a');\n    a.href = url;\n    a.download = filename;\n    document.body.appendChild(a);\n    a.click();\n    document.body.removeChild(a);\n    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);\n\n    localStorage.removeItem('pkm-autosave');\n    showNotification(`âœ… Note saved: ${filename}`);\n    lastSaved.textContent = `Saved at ${now.toLocaleTimeString()}`;\n\n    if (confirm('Note saved! Clear editor for new note?')) {\n        clearEditor();\n    }\n}\nSupprime les fonctions initVault() et configureVault() (plus nÃ©cessaires)\nChange le footer en :\nhtml<div class=\"footer-actions\">\n    <button class=\"btn-primary\" onclick=\"saveNote()\">ğŸ’¾ Save Note</button>\n</div>\n\n2. Simplifier le save (5 min)\nRemplace dans index.html :\nLa fonction saveNote() par cette version clean :\njavascript// Save note (simplified download)\nfunction saveNote() {\n    const content = editor.value;\n    if (!content.trim()) {\n        alert('Nothing to save!');\n        return;\n    }\n\n    const now = new Date();\n    const timestamp = now.toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace('T', '_').replace(/:/g, '-');\n    \n    // Extract title from first heading\n    const firstLine = content.split('\\n')[0];\n    let title = 'note';\n    if (firstLine.startsWith('#')) {\n        title = firstLine.replace(/^#+\\s*/, '').trim()\n            .toLowerCase()\n            .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')\n            .substring(0, 50);\n    }\n    \n    const filename = `${timestamp}_${title}.md`;\n\n    // Download file\n    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/markdown' });\n    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);\n    const a = document.createElement('a');\n    a.href = url;\n    a.download = filename;\n    document.body.appendChild(a);\n    a.click();\n    document.body.removeChild(a);\n    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);\n\n    localStorage.removeItem('pkm-autosave');\n    showNotification(`âœ… Note saved: ${filename}`);\n    lastSaved.textContent = `Saved at ${now.toLocaleTimeString()}`;\n\n    if (confirm('Note saved! Clear editor for new note?')) {\n        clearEditor();\n    }\n}\nSupprime les fonctions initVault() et configureVault() (plus nÃ©cessaires)\nChange le footer en :\nhtml<div class=\"footer-actions\">\n    <button class=\"btn-primary\" onclick=\"saveNote()\">ğŸ’¾ Save Note</button>\n</div>\n\n2. require('electron');\nconst path = require('path');\n\nlet mainWindow = null;\nlet captureWindow = null;\nlet referenceWindow = null;\nlet tray = null;\n\n// Create main hub window\nfunction createMainWindow() {\n    mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({\n        width: 600,\n        height: 700,\n        webPreferences: {\n            nodeIntegration: false,\n            contextIsolation: true,\n            preload: path.join(__dirname, '../preload/preload.js')\n        },\n        frame: true\n    });\n\n    mainWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, '../renderer/hub.html'));\n\n    mainWindow.on('closed', () => {\n        mainWindow = null;\n    });\n}\n\n// Create Quick Capture window\nfunction createCaptureWindow() {\n    if (captureWindow) {\n        captureWindow.focus();\n        return;\n    }\n\n    captureWindow = new BrowserWindow({\n        width: 900,\n        height: 700,\n        webPreferences: {\n            nodeIntegration: false,\n            contextIsolation: true,\n            preload: path.join(__dirname, '../preload/preload.js')\n        },\n        frame: true\n    });\n\n    captureWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, '../renderer/capture.html'));\n\n    captureWindow.on('closed', () => {\n        captureWindow = null;\n    });\n}\n\n// Create Quick Reference window\nfunction createReferenceWindow() {\n    if (referenceWindow) {\n        referenceWindow.focus();\n        return;\n    }\n\n    referenceWindow = new BrowserWindow({\n        width: 700,\n        height: 800,\n        webPreferences: {\n            nodeIntegration: false,\n            contextIsolation: true,\n            preload: path.join(__dirname, '../preload/preload.js')\n        },\n        frame: true\n    });\n\n    referenceWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, '../renderer/reference.html'));\n\n    referenceWindow.on('closed', () => {\n        referenceWindow = null;\n    });\n}\n\n// Create system tray\nfunction createTray() {\n    const iconPath = path.join(__dirname, '../../build/icon.png');\n    \n    // Skip tray if icon doesn't exist (we'll add it later)\n    try {\n        tray = new Tray(iconPath);\n        \n        const contextMenu = Menu.buildFromTemplate([\n            { label: 'ğŸ§  PKM System', enabled: false },\n            { type: 'separator' },\n            { label: 'ğŸ  Hub', click: () => mainWindow ? mainWindow.show() : createMainWindow() },\n            { label: 'âœï¸ Quick Capture', click: createCaptureWindow },\n            { label: 'âš¡ Quick Reference', click: createReferenceWindow },\n            { type: 'separator' },\n            { label: 'Quit', click: () => app.quit() }\n        ]);\n\n        tray.setToolTip('PKM System');\n        tray.setContextMenu(contextMenu);\n    } catch (err) {\n        console.log('Tray icon not found, skipping tray');\n    }\n}\n\n// Register global shortcuts\nfunction registerShortcuts() {\n    globalShortcut.register('CommandOrControl+Shift+Space', () => {\n        if (captureWindow) {\n            captureWindow.isVisible() ? captureWindow.hide() : captureWindow.show();\n        } else {\n            createCaptureWindow();\n        }\n    });\n\n    globalShortcut.register('CommandOrControl+Shift+F', () => {\n        if (referenceWindow) {\n            referenceWindow.isVisible() ? referenceWindow.hide() : referenceWindow.show();\n        } else {\n            createReferenceWindow();\n        }\n    });\n\n    console.log('âœ… Global shortcuts registered!');\n}\n\n// IPC handler for saving notes\nipcMain.handle('save-note', async (event, { filename, content }) => {\n    const fs = require('fs').promises;\n    const { dialog } = require('electron');\n    \n    try {\n        const result = await dialog.showOpenDialog({\n            properties: ['openDirectory'],\n            title: 'Select Vault Directory'\n        });\n\n        if (result.canceled) return { success: false };\n\n        const vaultPath = result.filePaths[0];\n        const inboxPath = path.join(vaultPath, '00_Inbox');\n        \n        await fs.mkdir(inboxPath, { recursive: true });\n        await fs.writeFile(path.join(inboxPath, filename), content, 'utf8');\n\n        return { success: true };\n    } catch (error) {\n        return { success: false, error: error.message };\n    }\n});\n\napp.whenReady().then(() => {\n    createMainWindow();\n    createTray();\n    registerShortcuts();\n});\n\napp.on('window-all-closed', () => {\n    // Keep running on Windows/Linux\n});\n\napp.on('will-quit', () => {\n    globalShortcut.unregisterAll();\n});\n\nconsole.log('ğŸ§  PKM System Starting...');\n\nğŸš€ RELANCE\npowershellnpm start\nÃ‡a devrait marcher Clear editor for new note?')) {\n                    clearEditor();\n                }\n            } else {\n                alert('Error saving note. Try again.');\n            }\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error('Save error:', error);\n            alert('Error saving note.');\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Fallback to download if not in Electron\n        downloadNote();\n    }\n}\n\n---\n\n## ğŸ¤– Message 640 - API Node.js pour l'app\njavascript// server/ai-engine.js\n\nconst { Ollama } = require('ollama');\nconst ollama = new Ollama();\n\nclass LocalAI {\n  \n  async analyzeTags(noteContent) {\n    const prompt = `\n      Analyse cette note et gÃ©nÃ¨re des tags pertinents.\n      Note : ${noteContent}\n      \n      Retourne uniquement une liste de tags sÃ©parÃ©s par des virgules.\n    `;\n    \n    const response = await ollama.generate({\n      model: 'llama3.1',\n      prompt: prompt,\n      stream: false\n    });\n    \n    return response.response.split(',').map(t => t.trim());\n  }\n  \n  async detectEmotions(noteContent) {\n    const prompt = `\n      DÃ©tecte les Ã©motions prÃ©sentes dans ce texte.\n      Texte : ${noteContent}\n      \n      Retourne uniquement les Ã©motions sous forme de liste.\n    `;\n    \n    const response = await ollama.generate({\n      model: 'llama3.1',\n      prompt: prompt\n    });\n    \n    return this.parseEmotions(response.response);\n  }\n  \n  async naturalLanguageSearch(query, notes) {\n    // Utilise embeddings pour recherche sÃ©mantique\n    const queryEmbedding = await this.embed(query);\n    \n    const results = notes.map(note => ({\n      note,\n      similarity: this.cosineSimilarity(queryEmbedding, note.embedding)\n    }))\n    .sort((a, b) => b.similarity - a.similarity)\n    .slice(0, 10);\n    \n    return results;\n  }\n}\n3. API Node.js pour l'app\njavascript// server/ai-engine.js\n\nconst { Ollama } = require('ollama');\nconst ollama = new Ollama();\n\nclass LocalAI {\n  \n  async analyzeTags(noteContent) {\n    const prompt = `\n      Analyse cette note et gÃ©nÃ¨re des tags pertinents.\n      Note : ${noteContent}\n      \n      Retourne uniquement une liste de tags sÃ©parÃ©s par des virgules.\n    `;\n    \n    const response = await ollama.generate({\n      model: 'llama3.1',\n      prompt: prompt,\n      stream: false\n    });\n    \n    return response.response.split(',').map(t => t.trim());\n  }\n  \n  async detectEmotions(noteContent) {\n    const prompt = `\n      DÃ©tecte les Ã©motions prÃ©sentes dans ce texte.\n      Texte : ${noteContent}\n      \n      Retourne uniquement les Ã©motions sous forme de liste.\n    `;\n    \n    const response = await ollama.generate({\n      model: 'llama3.1',\n      prompt: prompt\n    });\n    \n    return this.parseEmotions(response.response);\n  }\n  \n  async naturalLanguageSearch(query, notes) {\n    // Utilise embeddings pour recherche sÃ©mantique\n    const queryEmbedding = await this.embed(query);\n    \n    const results = notes.map(note => ({\n      note,\n      similarity: this.cosineSimilarity(queryEmbedding, note.embedding)\n    }))\n    .sort((a, b) => b.similarity - a.similarity)\n    .slice(0, 10);\n    \n    return results;\n  }\n}\n3. le textarea)\nHors textarea â†’ Esc = Ne fait RIEN (pas de fermeture)\n\nDans capture.html, trouve le event listener Escape et REMPLACE par :\njavascript// Esc - Sort du mode Ã©dition (vim-like)\nif (Ctrl+1/2/3, Ctrl+B, etc.)\nPour revenir en Ã©dition â†’ Click dans textarea OU i (comme vim)\n\nBonus VIM-like - Appuyer i pour entrer en mode Ã©dition :\nDans app.html, ajoute :\njavascript// 'i' - document.querySelector('.view-page.active');\n    if (activePage && activePage.id === 'page-capture') {\n        // Message Ã  l'iframe pour focus\n        const iframe = activePage.querySelector('iframe');\n        if (iframe && iframe.contentWindow) {\n            iframe.contentWindow.postMessage({ type: 'focus-editor' }, '*');\n        }\n    }\n}\nEt dans keys - Navigation directe (Ctrl+Up/Down)\n    if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'ArrowDown') {\n        e.preventDefault();\n        selectedNavIndex = (selectedNavIndex + 1) % navItems.length;\n selectedNav.getAttribute('data-page');\n        navigateToPage(page);\n    }\n\n    // ? - Show shortcuts\n    if (e.key === '?' && !e.shiftKey) {\n        e.preventDefault();\n
